nistaraṅgaḥ svarūpātmā sarve dehe vyavasthitaḥ  sahajātyāṃ yadutpannaṃ sahajaṃ tat prakīrtitam svabhāvaṃ sahajaṃ proktaṃ sarvākāraikasaṃvaram  he ta tasmāt sahajaṃ jagatsarvaṃ sahajaṃ svarūpamucyate  he ta sahajakāyaḥ sa eva bhagavān mantranaye phalalakṣaṇe sahajānandaḥ sahajakāya ityukto grāhyagrāhakavarjito vijñānadharmatātīto bhavanirvāṇāpratiṣṭhito buddhānāṃ  samājo devīnāṃ saṃvaraśca  vi pra pṛ  sahajatanuḥ ādhyātmikā vidyā prajñāpāramitā prakṛtiprabhāsvarā mahāmudrā sahajānandarūpiṇī dharmadhātuniṣpandapūrṇāvasthā sahajatanurityucyate  se ṭī  pṛ  binduḥ śūnyo bhavati sa ca binduracyutaḥ san paramākṣara ucyate paramākṣaropyakāraḥ akārasaṃbhavaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ prajñopāyātmako vajrasattvo napuṃsakapadaṃ sahajakāya ityucyate sa ca kālacakro bhagavān paramākṣaraḥ sukhapadam  se ṭī pṛ saṃvaraḥsarvadhātūnāṃ samāhāro melāpakaḥ samājaḥ saṃvara iti  se ṭī pṛ bāhyānāmaudārikāṇāmadhyātmagataṃ yo yogī niścinuyāt tat teṣāṃ saṃvaramsaṃvṛtatvāt saṃkṣepavaratvāt  he ta ṭī pa asaṃvaraḥ sekaḥ  he ta ṭī pa asaṃvṛtiḥanuyogastu saṃvṛtiḥ  a kra vākprapañcastu saṃvṛtiḥ  a kra sādṛśyamsādṛśyaṃ yathā darpaṇārpitaṃ mukhasya pratibimbaṃ mukhaṃ na bhavati na pūrvaṃ siddhirnāpyadhunā siddhyati tadeva mukhapratibimbaṃ sādṛśyamātramāpādayatitathāpi lokāḥ svamukhaṃ dṛṣṭamiti kṛtvā bhrāntyā santuṣṭā bhavanti  a va saṃ pṛ sādhumatīaṅgulīpādapṛṣṭhe śmaśānamsarvapīṭhātmatvādvikalpapadānubhūteśca saiva sādhumatīsādhuno nairātmyasya tatra vidyamānatvāt  vi ti ṭī pṛ sāmānyādhātusāmyasya śleṣmaṇo vahanāt sāmānyā guhye  va ti ṭī pṛ sālijammahāmāṃsaṃ sālijaṃ proktam  he ta siddhāsvedotpādaḥ samāpattau sarvatra siddhaḥ tadvāhitvāt siddhā jaṅghayoḥsiddhanimittotpādanaṃ prati vā tadadhikārāt  va ti ṭī pṛ siddhiḥlaukikasiddhirityakaniṣṭhabhuvanaparyantādhipatyam uttarasiddhiriti savāsanasarvakleśajñeyasamāpattyāvaraṇaprahāṇito dvādaśabhūmipratilambhena samyaksaṃbuddhatvam  se ṭī pṛ siddhistraidhātukeśvaratvam  se pṛ trividhā siddhiruttamamadhyamādhamāḥ tatrāntardhānamuttamābhūgatanidhānadarśanaṃ madhyamāvaśīkaraṇamadhamā siddhiḥ  gu sa pra pṛ siddhyaṣṭakamañjanaguṭikāpādukāsiddhauṣadhimaṇimantrayakṣastrīparapurapraveśākhyam  ta saṃ ṭī pṛ sindhuḥsindhustu pādapṛṣṭhaṃ vai  va ti pṛ pādāpṛṣṭhādaṅguṣṭhe bodhicittasya spandanāt sindhuḥ pādapṛṣtham  va ti ṭī pṛ sindhau mahābalā khyātā saśokā cāśruvāhinī  va ti pṛ sihlakamsvavaymbhuḥ sihlakaṃ jñeyam  he ta sukhamsukhaṃ dvīndriyajaṃ tattvaṃ devānāṃ rāgiṇāṃ smṛtam trailokyācāranirmuktaṃ buddhānāṃ sukhamakṣaram hasitekṣaṇādibhirmuktaṃ sarvadvandvavivarjitam kāryakāraṇanirmuktaṃ trailokyābhāsamadvayam apratiṣṭhaṃ yathākāśaṃ vyāpi lakṣaṇavarjitam uktaṃ tatparaṃ tattvaṃ vajrajñānamanuttaram apratiṣṭhaṃ yathākāśaṃ vyāpi lakṣaṇavarjitam anirdeśyamarūpaṃ ca etattatvasya lakṣaṇam yadviśuddhamivākāśamajñānatimirākulaiḥ candrakairiva saṃchannaṃ vastubhirvedyate jinaiḥ  se ṭī pṛ sukhaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sukhaṃ pītaṃ sukhaṃ raktaṃ sukhaṃ sitam sukhaṃ śyāmaṃ sukhaṃ nīlaṃ sukhaṃ kṛtsnaṃ carācaram sukhaṃ prajñā sukhopāyaḥ sukhaṃ kundurujaṃ tathā sukhaṃ bhāvaḥ sukhābhāvo vajrasattvaḥ sukhaḥ smṛtaḥ  he sukhāvatīamitābhasya tathāgatasya buddhakṣetraṃ sukhāvatītyucyate iha tu nairātmyādīnāṃ bhagāni sukhāvatīsaṃkṣepāṇiniruttarasukhasya rakṣaṇāt  he ta ṭī pa bviharehaṃ sukhāvatyāṃ sadvajrayoṣito bhage ekārākṛtirūpe tu buddharatnakaraṇḍake  he ta yoṣidbhage sukhāvatyām  he ta strīkakkolasukhāvatyāmevaṃkārasvarūpake sukhasya rakṣaṇādeva sukhāvatīti śabditam he ta sucandraḥ śītānadyuttare ṣaṇṇavatikoṭigrāmaśambhalamahāviṣayādhipatirdevāsuranāganirmāṇakāyaiḥ ṣaṇṇavatimahārājakulaprasūtairmahāratnamukuṭabaddhaiḥ  koṭikoṭigrāmādhipatibhirnamaskṛtacaraṇāravindaḥ sarvasattvabhāṣāntaraistathāgatoktadharmāṇāṃ saṃgrāhakatvena sarvatathāgataśrotṛtvāt ṣoḍaśakalāvaraṇaprahāṇyā  candravimalaprabhātvācca śobhanaścāsau candraśceti sucandro guhyādhipatirāḍhakavatīnivāsī śrīvajrapāṇiḥ  se ṭī pṛ  tannirmāṇakāyaḥ sucandro rājādhyeṣayati taduktaṃ mūlatantratrailokyanāyakaṃ buddhaṃ bodhisattvāmarādayaḥ svasvāsane niṣaṇṇāste mantrayānaśrutārthinaḥ dīpaṅkareṇa yā pūrvaṃ mantrayānasya deśanā kṛtāsmākaṃ tu kartavyā gautamenādya sādhunā athātaḥ śambhalākhyāto vajrapāṇivinirmitaḥ sucandranṛpa āyātaḥ saddharmaśrīdharmadhātukam ādau pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā śāstuḥ pādāmbujadvayam ratnapuṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā saṃbuddhasyāgrataḥ sthitaḥ tatnrasyādhyeṣakaḥ śāstuscandraḥ saṃgītikārakaḥ se ṭī pṛ vajrayāne aḍakavatīnivāsī mahāyakṣādhipatirmahābodhisattvo vajrapāṇistathāgatasyādhyeṣakaḥ saṃgītikāraśca kathaṃ sambhalaviṣayakalāpagrāmamādhipateḥ sūryaprabhasya vijayādevīgarbhasambhūtaḥ sucandro rājādhyeṣakaḥ  vi pra pṛ  sudurjayāmukhakaṇṭhau chandohaurasopabhoge chandavṛtteḥ saiva sudurjayārasānnivartayitumaśakyatvāt  va ti ṭī pṛ subhadraḥsukhādāpyāyikāguṇavartipravartakatvāt subhadraḥ  va ṭi ṭī pṛ subhadrāśobhanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ bhadraṃ kalyāṇaṃ yasyāḥ sā subhadrā  va ti ṭī pṛ prajñābalaṃ subhadrā  va ti pṛ sumanāḥkheṭena yogināṃ saumanasyajananāt sumanāḥ pādapṛṣṭhe  va ti ṭī pṛ surābhakṣīsurāṃ sudhāṃ bhakṣayatīti surābhakṣījñānolau  va ti ṭī pṛ smṛtibalaṃ surābhakṣī  va ti pṛ surāvairīsurāṇāṃ snāyūnāṃ vairī vāmakarṇāt pravartakaḥ surāvairī  va ti ṭī pṛ suvarṇadvīpamsuvarṇasya susitatviṣaścittasya dvīpamiva dvīpaṃ jaṅghādvayamevaitat  va ti ṭī pṛ jaṅghādvayaṃ tu vikhyātaṃ suvarṇadvīpasaṃjñakam  va ti pṛ prasvedavāhinī nāḍī suvarṇadvīpasaṃsthitā samākulā sudīptāṅgī matā sā cakravarmiṇī  va ti pṛ suvīrāsuṣṭhu virādakārāt prabhavatīti suvīrā  va ti ṭī pṛ upekṣāsambodhyaṅgaṃ suvīrā va ti pṛ sūkṣmākeśaromṇāṃ susūkṣmāṇāṃ vahanāt sūkṣmarūpā śikhāyām  va ti ṭī pṛ sūtrāntam sautrāntikaḥsūtrāntamiti anaghigambhīrāṇi sūtrāṇi sūtrāntāni ekagāthācaturgāthāupadhāriṇīṣaṇmukhībhadracaryālalitavistaradaśabhūmikādīni he ta ṭī pa basūryamsūryam utpādādvayajñānam  ca ko vyā pṛ sūryaḥsūryaśabdena prāṇavāyuḥ  vi pra pṛ atreḍāpiṅgalāsuṣumnānāmadhipatiḥ prāṇaḥ sūryo nābherūrdhvaṃ pravāhataḥ  vi pra pṛ sūryanāḍī rasanānābherūrdhvaṃ tu yā nāḍī vahatyūrdhvamukhī tathā kaṇṭhamadhye tu viśrāntā raktavahā prakīrtitā  va ti pṛ yeyaṃ dakṣiṇapārśve rasanākhyā nāḍīsā ūrdhvamukhī nābherārabhya kaṇṭhaṃ yāvad raktaṃ vahati  va ti ṭī pṛ sekaḥsicyate kāyādikaṃ nirmalaṃ nirāvaraṇaṃ kriyateneneti sekaḥ  se ṭī pṛ ḍākinīvajrapañjarepyekādaśaiva sekā uktāḥ  tathāhiprathamaṃ toyasekena dvitīyaṃ maulisekataḥ tṛtīyaṃ paṭṭasekena caturthaṃ vajraghaṇṭayā pañcamaṃ svādhipenaiva nāmasekaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam buddhājñā saptamaṃ sekaṃ kalaśaṃ sekamaṣṭamam navamaṃ guhyasekena daśamaṃ prajñābhiṣekataḥ tattvavajraprayogeṇa sarvān vajrapadān dadet vyākaroti svayaṃ śāstā eṣa sekavidhiṃ svayam ācāryo nāvamantavyaḥ sugatājñāṃ na laṅghayet  iti se ṭī pṛ  evamekādaśobhiṣekaḥ pradhānastattvavajraprayogeṇeti bhagavato viṣpaṣṭavacanāccaturtho vaikādaśo vābhiṣekaḥ pṛthag nāvagantavyo vidvadbhiriti   se ṭī pṛ  yathāsaṃkhyameṣāṃ kumbhādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ sānvayāni kṣarākṣaraspandanispandākhyāni nāmāni tathā bālaprauḍhavṛddhaprajāpatisaṃjñakāni  caturdaloṣṇīṣapadmāt śukrāmṛtadhārāyāḥ ṣoḍaśadalalalāṭe kamalakarṇikāyāmāgamanena yat kāyānandavāgānandacittānandajñānānandātmakaṃ sukhānubhavanaṃ  tad bālam  prathamasekaprāptatvād yogī payodharābhiṣikto bāla ityucyate tatastasyā bhage īṣadvajroddolanena bodhicittacyutamiti  dvātriṃśaddalakarakamalādaṣṭadalahṛtkamalakarṇikāyāṃ yatkāyaparamānandavākparamānandacittaparamānandajñānaparamānandātmakaṃ sukhānubhavanaṃ  tat pūrvādatiricyamānatvāt proḍhau guhyābhiṣekaḥ   tato gāḍhoddolanena spandaṃ gata iti catuḥṣaṣṭidalanābhikamaladvātriṃśaddalaguhyakamalāgamanena śukrendoḥ pañcadaśakamalasyāgragasvacchadravasya  spandākhyasya vajramaṇisuṣiraparyantāgamanena yadadhimātraṃ kāyaviramānandavāgviramānandacittaviramānandajñānaviramānandātmakaṃ sukhānubhavanaṃ  sa vṛddhaḥ prajñājñānābhiṣekaḥ  mahāmudreti gaganodbhavabimbam  tasyāḥ svarasabāhyabhāvanākhyānurāgājjātaṃ nispandata iti niruddho vajramaṇerbāhyaspando bhagecyutasukhatayā yasya candrāmṛtasya sa kāyasahajānandavāksahajānandacittasahajānandajñānasahajānandātmako  mahājñānākhyaścaturthaḥ sekaḥ   asau nirāvaraṇalokottarajñānādhigataḥ siddharasavat tāmrādidhātūnāṃ svarṇabhāveneva sāvaraṇaskandhadhātvādīnāṃ pañcatathāgatapañcadevatādirpajābhāvena  niṣpādakatvāt prajāpatiḥ  se ṭī pṛ  bāhyavāriṇeva bāhyamalasya avidyāmalakṣālanāya sicyateneneti sekaḥ  a va saṃ pṛ saṃvaraḥ sekaḥ tathā ca vakṣyatisekaṃ caturvidhaṃ khyātaṃ sattvānāṃ hitahetave sicyate snāpyatenena sekastenābhidhīyate   he ta ṭī pa a sekāsiñcati hṛdayān sudhāraseneti sekā bāhumūladvaye  va ti ṭī pṛ  sevābodhiliṅgālambanaṃ sevā  gu sa pra pṛ sevyate mumukṣubhirabhyasyata iti sevā  gu sa pra pṛ uttamasādhanasthānāṃ tu vajracatuṣkaṃ śūnyatācatuṣṭayamtena sevā kāryā  gu sa pra pṛ saukhyambodhicittādṛte nānyat saukhyamasti tridhātukebodhicittamayaṃ saukhyaṃ sarvasaukhyaprasarpaṇam jñā si pṛ saurāṣṭramūrū saurāṣṭra ucyate  va ti pṛ saukhyasya rāṣṭramviśiṣṭakāladarśane ca ūrudvayamevānyonyam  va ti pṛ saurāṣṭre lohitākhyā tu śaūṇdinī ḍākinī matā  va ti ṭī pṛ stambhaḥstambho nāma devatāveśāt pūrvaṃ pātrasya prākṛtāhaṅkāramapanīya stimitabhāvena kāṣṭhavat sthityavasthā stambhanam  gu sa pra pṛ stobhaḥstobhamutpatanakampanabhramaṇam  gu sa pra pṛ sthaviraḥsthaviro yo daśavarṣopapannaḥ  do ko vyā pṛ smṛtīndriyamvīryendriyodānitān dharmān yena punaḥ punarāmukhīkriyantena vismaryantetat smṛtīndriyam  va ti ṭī pṛ smṛtyupasthānānikāyānusmṛtivedanasmṛticittānusmṛtidharmānusmṛtināmakāni catvāri smṛtyupasthānāni śrāvakadarśane tu nityasukhaśucisātmakacaturviparyāsapratipakṣānityāśuciduḥkhānātmalakṣaṇāni catvāri smṛtyupasthānānīti viśeṣaḥ mantradarśane tu svasaṃvidrūpā ḍākinyaḥ kāyādīnāṃ dharmatārūpā jñeyāḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ sruksurvausruvaṃ tu rasanākhyātā hṛccandro lalanātmakaḥ  va ti pṛ vāmadakṣiṇage lalanārasane adhodravyavāhitvātvād yathākramaṃ sruksruvau jñeyau  va ti ṭī pṛ svabhāvaḥsvabhāvaścaivānādyanutpannaṃ na satyaṃ na mṛṣeti ca pañcākārāṇāṃ pratītyasamutpannānāṃ pañcatathāgatasvabhāvatvamsvabhāvasya ca śūnyatākaruṇābhinnatvād śūnyatākaruṇābhinnaṃjagaditi sthitam  pratītyasambhavādeva gandharvapuravat sphuṭam na svabhāvasthitaṃ viśvaṃ nākāśāmbhojasaṃnibham uktaṃ ca hevajre   amī dharmāstu nirvāṇaṃ mohāt saṃsārarūpiṇaḥ  a va saṃ pṛ svabhāvakāyaḥdvātriṃśattu dalaṃ padmaṃ mūrdhni madhye vyavasthitam  va ti pṛ śiraścakraṃ mahājñānaṃ svabhāvakāyaḥpāramārthikabodhicittasvarūpatvāt  va ti ṭī pṛ dvātriṃśacchadake tathā mahāsukhamahājñānaṃ samantāt saṃvyavasthitam  va ti pṛ mahāsukhamahācakre haṃkāro bindurūpakaḥ  va ti pṛ svādhiṣṭhānamsvādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma saṃvṛteḥ satyadarśanam  se ṭī pṛ  māyāsvapnagandharvapurapratisenādivadakalpitaśeṣaskandhadhātvāyatanādidarśanaṃ saṃvṛtisatyadarśanaṃ svādhiṣṭhānaṃ cocyate  se ṭī pṛ  svādhiṣṭhānaṃ śūnye traidhātukadarśanaṃ nāma  vi pra pṛ svāhāsvāheti mantradevatāsamāśvāsanam  gu sa pra pṛ haṭhayogaḥidānīṃ haṭhayoga ucyate  iha yadā pratyāhārādibhirbimbe dṛṣṭe satyapyakṣarakṣaṇaṃ notpadyateyantritaprāṇatayā tadā nādābhyāsāddhaṭhena prāṇaṃ madhyamāyāṃ vāhayitvā  prajñābjagatakuliśamaṇau bodhicittabindunirodhādakṣarakṣaṇaṃ sādhayenniṣpandeneti haṭhayogaḥ  nādābhyāsotraivokaḥ  se ṭī pṛ hayakarṇāhayavaddakṣiṇakarṇena nirgacchatīti hayakarṇā  va ti ṭī pṛ samādhisambodhyaṅgaṃ hayakarṇā  va ti pṛ hayagrīvaḥurubhyāṃ balavato raktasya pravartanād hayagrīvaḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ hariṇīṣaḍ viṣayān bhavagrahān harati khaṇḍayatīti hariṇī sandhyābhāṣayā saiva jñānamudrā  ca ko vyā pṛ havirbhājanamśiraḥkapālametattu havirbhājanamucyate  va ti pṛ yadetacchiraḥkapālaṃ mūrdhni kapālamtadeva candrājyahaviṣa ādhārabhūtatvāddhavirbhājanaṃ nānyat  va ti ṭī pṛ sīmāntamadhyagā cāpi himālaye khagānanā  va ti pṛ hūṃkāraḥmadhyavṛtterniruttaradharmatāsūcako hūṃkāraḥ tasyārthaḥha iti hetuviyuktaḥū iti ūhāpagataḥa iti apratiṣṭhitasarvadharma iti  a va saṃ pṛ hṛdvajraḥsarvatathāgatāḥ proktāḥ pañcaskandhā jinairiha tadātmakāyavākcitto hṛdvajrosau mahāsukhaḥ  gu sa pra pṛ hṛṣṭavadanāsīmanto varaṭakamadhyastadvāhitvād hṛṣṭavadanāt karasparśāt prajñopāyayoḥ sānandanandanatvānmeḍhre  va ti ṭī pṛ hetudāyikāgātrapuṣṭau meda eva hetustadvahanāddhetudāyikā pādāṅgulīṣu  va ti ṭī herukamśūnyāśūnyaṃ tu herukam  he ta  śūnyāśūnyaṃ prajñopāyayorekarasarūpatvāt etadeva jñānaṃ herukaśabdavācyamśūnyatākaruṇayoradvayarūpatvāt he ta ṭī pa abherukaḥsarvarūpastu herukaḥ  va ti pṛ sarveṣāṃ pañcaskandhānāṃrūpaṃ sahajātmakamasyāstīti sarvarūpī vyāpako yaḥ sa śrīheruko bhagavān ṣaṣṭho mahāvajradharaḥdharmatāsvabhāvo vijñeya iti śeṣaḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ sarvāyatanadhātustu herukaḥ parameśvaraḥ  va ti pṛ kaṅkālo daṇḍarūposau herukaḥ paramāśrayaḥ skandhadhātvādibuddhānāṃ stūpa ityabhidhīyate  va ti ṭī pṛ samyaksamādhirbhagavān śrīherukaḥ  va ti pṛ eṣa śrīheruko vīro vasantatilakā smṛtā  va ti pṛ tatra nirmāṇacakre nābhau sa eva vasantokāro hrasvarūpaḥ hṛdi dharmacakre nādabinduyuktahūṃkārākāraḥ saṃbhogacakre kaṇṭhe sa eva trimātraḥ plutaḥ praṇavarūpaḥ nāḍīkauṭilyāt tasya triparivartaścaṇḍālyāḥ praveśānnirgamācceti kṛtvā lalāṭe mahāsukhacakre bindunādavibhūṣitonāhatākṣaro haṃkāraḥ tadeva vilomena śiraḥkaṇṭhahṛdayanābhirūpaḥ śrīheruko mantramūrtiḥ  va tiṭī pṛ pādāṅgulibhyobhedyahūkārarūpasya medasaḥ pravartakatvāt śrīherukaḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ kāyatrayasvabhāvo bhagavān śrīherukaḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ hevajramhekāreṇa mahākaruṇā vajraṃ prajñā ca bhaṇyate prajñopāyātmakaṃ tantram  he ta hekāramiti mahākaruṇāmvajraṃ sarvadharmaśūnyatām  he ta ṭī pa bhomaḥprajñāgnau caṇḍālījvalanatīkṣṇatvāt dāhojjvale homosau vijñeyaḥ  va ti ṭī pṛ ābhyantaraistu śukrādyairbāhyaiḥ rūpādibhistathā havibhiḥ kriyate homaḥ prajñāgnau tu mahojjvale  va ti pṛ  END
